### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-628">Log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core (servizio app Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-628">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-629">Il log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core spesso registra utili messaggi di errore non disponibili nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-629">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-630">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-630">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-631">Passare al pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** nel portale di Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-631">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-632">In **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY** (SELEZIONARE LA CATEGORIA DEL PROBLEMA) selezionare il pulsante **Web App Down** (App Web inattiva).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-632">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY** , select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-633">In **Suggested Solutions (Soluzioni consigliate)** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection** (Abilita il reindirizzamento del log Stdout) selezionare il pulsante **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config** (Apri la console Kudu per modificare Web.Config).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-633">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection** , select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-634">Nella **console diagnostica** Kudu aprire le cartelle nel percorso **site** > **wwwroot** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-634">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console** , open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-635">Scorrere verso il basso fino a visualizzare il file *web.config* in fondo all'elenco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-635">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-636">Fare clic sull'icona della matita accanto al file *web.config* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-636">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-637">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `true` e cambiare il percorso di **stdoutLogFile** in: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-637">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-638">Selezionare **Salva** per salvare il file *web.config* aggiornato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-638">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-639">Effettuare una richiesta all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-639">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-640">Tornare al portale di Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-640">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-641">Selezionare il pannello **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **STRUMENTI DI SVILUPPO** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-641">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-642">Selezionare il **pulsante &rarr; Vai** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-642">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-643">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-643">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-644">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-644">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-645">Selezionare la cartella **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-645">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-646">Controllare la colonna **Data modifica** e selezionare l'icona della matita per modificare il log stdout con la data di modifica più recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-646">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-647">Quando si apre il file di log, verrà visualizzato l'errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-647">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-648">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, disabilitare la registrazione stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-648">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-649">Nella **console diagnostica** Kudu tornare al percorso **site** > **wwwroot** per visualizzare il file *web.config* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-649">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console** , return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-650">Aprire nuovamente il file **web.config** selezionando l'icona della matita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-650">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-651">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-651">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-652">Selezionare **Salva** per salvare il file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-652">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-653">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-653">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-654">La mancata disabilitazione del log stdout può causare un errore dell'app o del server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-654">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-655">Non esiste alcun limite per le dimensioni dei file di log o il numero di file di log che è possibile creare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-655">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-656">Usare la registrazione stdout solo per la risoluzione dei problemi di avvio delle app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-656">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-657">Per la registrazione generale in un'app ASP.NET Core dopo l'avvio, usare una libreria di registrazione che limita le dimensioni dei file di log e ne esegue la rotazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-657">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-658">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Provider di registrazione di terze parti](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-658">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-659">Log di debug del modulo ASP.NET Core (servizio app Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-659">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-660">Il log di debug del modulo ASP.NET Core fornisce dati di registrazione aggiuntivi e più approfonditi dal modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-660">The ASP.NET Core Module debug log provides additional, deeper logging from the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-661">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-661">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-662">Per abilitare il log di diagnostica avanzato, eseguire le operazioni seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-662">To enable the enhanced diagnostic log, perform either of the following:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-663">Seguire le istruzioni in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) per configurare l'app per la registrazione di diagnostica avanzata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-663">Follow the instructions in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to configure the app for an enhanced diagnostic logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-664">Ridistribuire l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-664">Redeploy the app.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-665">Aggiungere le impostazioni `<handlerSettings>` indicate in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) al file *web.config* dell'app distribuita, usando la console Kudu:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-665">Add the `<handlerSettings>` shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to the live app's *web.config* file using the Kudu console:</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-666">Aprire **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **Strumenti di sviluppo** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-666">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-667">Selezionare il **pulsante &rarr; Vai** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-667">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-668">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-668">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-669">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-669">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD** .</span></span>
     1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-670">Aprire le cartelle nel **sito** del percorso  >  **wwwroot** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-670">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-671">Modificare il file *web.config* selezionando il pulsante a forma di matita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-671">Edit the *web.config* file by selecting the pencil button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-672">Aggiungere la sezione `<handlerSettings>` come illustrato in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-672">Add the `<handlerSettings>` section as shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-673">Fare clic sul pulsante **Salva** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-673">Select the **Save** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-674">Aprire **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **Strumenti di sviluppo** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-674">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-675">Selezionare il **pulsante &rarr; Vai** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-675">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-676">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-676">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-678">Aprire le cartelle nel **sito** del percorso  >  **wwwroot** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-678">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot** .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-679">Se non è stato specificato un percorso per il file *aspnetcore-debug.log* , il file viene visualizzato nell'elenco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-679">If you didn't supply a path for the *aspnetcore-debug.log* file, the file appears in the list.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-680">Se è stato specificato un percorso, passare al percorso del file di log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-680">If you supplied a path, navigate to the location of the log file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-683">Per disabilitare il log di debug avanzato, eseguire le operazioni seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-683">To disable the enhanced debug log, perform either of the following:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-687">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-687">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-688">La mancata disabilitazione del log di debug può causare un errore dell'app o del server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-688">Failure to disable the debug log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-689">Non è previsto alcun limite per le dimensioni del file di log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-689">There's no limit on log file size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-690">Usare solo la registrazione di debug per la risoluzione dei problemi di avvio delle app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-690">Only use debug logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>

### <a name="monitoring-blades"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-697">Pannelli di monitoraggio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-697">Monitoring blades</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-698">I pannelli di monitoraggio forniscono un'esperienza di risoluzione dei problemi alternativa ai metodi descritti in precedenza in questo argomento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-698">Monitoring blades provide an alternative troubleshooting experience to the methods described earlier in the topic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-699">È possibile usare questi pannelli per diagnosticare gli errori della serie 500.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-699">These blades can be used to diagnose 500-series errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-700">Verificare che le estensioni di ASP.NET Core siano installate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-700">Confirm that the ASP.NET Core Extensions are installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-701">Se le estensioni non sono installate, installarle manualmente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-701">If the extensions aren't installed, install them manually:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-713">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-713">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD** .</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-725">Nei dati del flusso di registrazione viene indicata la causa dell'errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-725">Within the log stream data, the cause of the error is indicated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-726">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, assicurarsi di disabilitare la registrazione stdout.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-726">Be sure to disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-727">Per visualizzare i log di traccia delle richieste non riuscite (log FREB):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-727">To view the failed request tracing logs (FREB logs):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-728">Passare al pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** nel portale di Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-728">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-730">Per altre informazioni, vedere la [sezione relativa alla traccia delle richieste non riuscite nell'argomento Abilitare la registrazione diagnostica per le app Web nel servizio app di Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) e [Domande frequenti sulle prestazioni delle applicazioni in App Web di Azure: Come si abilita la traccia delle richieste non riuscite?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-730">See [Failed request traces section of the Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service topic](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) and the [Application performance FAQs for Web Apps in Azure: How do I turn on failed request tracing?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) for more information.</span></span>

>
> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-734">Per la registrazione di routine in un'app ASP.NET Core, usare una libreria di registrazione che limita le dimensioni dei file di log e ne esegue la rotazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-734">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-735">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Provider di registrazione di terze parti](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-735">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-736">Risolvere i problemi in IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-736">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>

### <a name="application-event-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-737">Registro eventi applicazioni (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-737">Application Event Log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-738">Accedere al log eventi dell'applicazione:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-738">Access the Application Event Log:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-739">Aprire il menu Start, cercare *Visualizzatore eventi* e selezionare l'app **Visualizzatore eventi** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-739">Open the Start menu, search for *Event Viewer* , and select the **Event Viewer** app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-740">In **Visualizzatore eventi** aprire il nodo **Registri di Windows** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-740">In **Event Viewer** , open the **Windows Logs** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-741">Selezionare **Applicazione** per aprire il log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-741">Select **Application** to open the Application Event Log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-742">Cercare gli errori associati all'app in cui si è verificato il problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-742">Search for errors associated with the failing app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-743">Gli errori presentano un valore *Modulo AspNetCore IIS* o *Modulo AspNetCore IIS Express* nella colonna *Origine* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-743">Errors have a value of *IIS AspNetCore Module* or *IIS Express AspNetCore Module* in the *Source* column.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-at-a-command-prompt"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-744">Eseguire l'app da un prompt dei comandi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-744">Run the app at a command prompt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-745">Molti errori di avvio non producono informazioni utili nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-745">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-746">È possibile individuare la causa di alcuni errori eseguendo l'app da un prompt dei comandi nel sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-746">You can find the cause of some errors by running the app at a command prompt on the hosting system.</span></span>

#### <a name="framework-dependent-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-747">Distribuzione dipendente dal framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-747">Framework-dependent deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-748">Se l'app è una [distribuzione dipendente dal framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-748">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-749">Da un prompt dei comandi passare alla cartella di distribuzione e avviare l'app eseguendo l'assembly dell'app con *dotnet.exe* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-749">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app by executing the app's assembly with *dotnet.exe* .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-750">Nel comando seguente sostituire il nome dell'assembly dell'app per \<assembly_name> : `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-750">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-751">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà scritto nella finestra della console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-751">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-752">Se gli errori si verificano quando si effettua una richiesta all'app, effettuare una richiesta all'host e alla porta su cui è in ascolto Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-752">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-753">Usando l'host e la porta predefiniti, effettuare una richiesta a `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-753">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-754">Se l'app risponde normalmente nell'indirizzo endpoint di Kestrel, è più probabile che il problema sia associato alla configurazione dell'host e che non sia interno all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-754">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

#### <a name="self-contained-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-755">Distribuzione autonoma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-755">Self-contained deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-756">Se l'app è una [distribuzione autonoma](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-756">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-757">Da un prompt dei comandi passare alla cartella di distribuzione e avviare il file eseguibile dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-757">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app's executable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-758">Nel comando seguente sostituire il nome dell'assembly dell'app per \<assembly_name> : `<assembly_name>.exe` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-758">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-759">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà scritto nella finestra della console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-759">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-760">Se gli errori si verificano quando si effettua una richiesta all'app, effettuare una richiesta all'host e alla porta su cui è in ascolto Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-760">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-761">Usando l'host e la porta predefiniti, effettuare una richiesta a `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-761">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-762">Se l'app risponde normalmente nell'indirizzo endpoint di Kestrel, è più probabile che il problema sia associato alla configurazione dell'host e che non sia interno all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-762">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-763">Log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-763">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-764">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-764">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-765">Passare alla cartella di distribuzione del sito nel sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-765">Navigate to the site's deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-766">Se la cartella *logs* non è presente, creare la cartella.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-766">If the *logs* folder isn't present, create the folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-767">Per istruzioni su come impostare MSBuild per la creazione automatica della cartella *logs* nella distribuzione, vedere l'argomento [Struttura della directory](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-767">For instructions on how to enable MSBuild to create the *logs* folder in the deployment automatically, see the [Directory structure](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure) topic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-768">Modificare il file *web.config* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-768">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-769">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `true` e modificare il percorso di **stdoutLogFile** in modo da fare riferimento alla cartella *logs* , ad esempio `.\logs\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-769">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to point to the *logs* folder (for example, `.\logs\stdout`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-770">`stdout` nel percorso è il prefisso del nome del file di log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-770">`stdout` in the path is the log file name prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-771">Un timestamp, l'ID del processo e l'estensione del file vengono aggiunti automaticamente al momento della creazione del log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-771">A timestamp, process id, and file extension are added automatically when the log is created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-772">Usando `stdout` come prefisso del nome del file, un tipico file di log è denominato *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-772">Using `stdout` as the file name prefix, a typical log file is named *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log* .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-773">Assicurarsi che l'identità del pool di applicazioni disponga delle autorizzazioni di scrittura per la cartella *logs* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-773">Ensure your application pool's identity has write permissions to the *logs* folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-774">Salvare il file *web.config* aggiornato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-774">Save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-775">Effettuare una richiesta all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-775">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-776">Passare alla cartella *logs* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-776">Navigate to the *logs* folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-777">Trovare e aprire il log stdout più recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-777">Find and open the most recent stdout log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-778">Esaminare il log per verificare se sono presenti errori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-778">Study the log for errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-779">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, disabilitare la registrazione stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-779">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-780">Modificare il file *web.config* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-780">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-781">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-781">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-782">Salvare il file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-782">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-783">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-783">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-784">La mancata disabilitazione del log stdout può causare un errore dell'app o del server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-784">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-785">Non esiste alcun limite per le dimensioni dei file di log o il numero di file di log che è possibile creare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-785">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-786">Per la registrazione di routine in un'app ASP.NET Core, usare una libreria di registrazione che limita le dimensioni dei file di log e ne esegue la rotazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-786">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-787">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Provider di registrazione di terze parti](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-787">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-788">Log di debug del modulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-788">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-789">Aggiungere le impostazioni del gestore seguenti al file di *web.config* dell'app per abilitare ASP.NET Core log di debug del modulo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-789">Add the following handler settings to the app's *web.config* file to enable ASP.NET Core Module debug log:</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore ...>
  <handlerSettings>
    <handlerSetting name="debugLevel" value="file" />
    <handlerSetting name="debugFile" value="c:\temp\ancm.log" />
  </handlerSettings>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-790">Verificare che il percorso specificato per il log esista e che l'identità del pool di applicazioni abbia le autorizzazioni di scrittura nel percorso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-790">Confirm that the path specified for the log exists and that the app pool's identity has write permissions to the location.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-791">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-791">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-developer-exception-page"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-792">Abilitare la pagina delle eccezioni per gli sviluppatori</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-792">Enable the Developer Exception Page</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-793">La variabile di ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [ può essere aggiunta a web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) per eseguire l'app nell'ambiente di sviluppo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-793">The `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [environment variable can be added to web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) to run the app in the Development environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-794">Purché l'ambiente non sia sottoposto a override durante l'avvio dell'app tramite `UseEnvironment` nel generatore di host, l'impostazione della variabile di ambiente consente di visualizzare la [pagina delle eccezioni per gli sviluppatori](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) quando viene eseguita l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-794">As long as the environment isn't overridden in app startup by `UseEnvironment` on the host builder, setting the environment variable allows the [Developer Exception Page](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) to appear when the app is run.</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore processPath="dotnet"
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll"
      stdoutLogEnabled="false"
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout"
      hostingModel="InProcess">
  <environmentVariables>
    <environmentVariable name="ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT" value="Development" />
  </environmentVariables>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-795">L'impostazione della variabile di ambiente per `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` è consigliata solo per l'uso in server di gestione temporanea e test non esposti a Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-795">Setting the environment variable for `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` is only recommended for use on staging and testing servers that aren't exposed to the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-796">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, rimuovere la variabile di ambiente dal file *web.config* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-796">Remove the environment variable from the *web.config* file after troubleshooting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-797">Per informazioni sull'impostazione delle variabili di ambiente in *web.config* , vedere [elemento figlio environmentVariables di aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-797">For information on setting environment variables in *web.config* , see [environmentVariables child element of aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span></span>

### <a name="obtain-data-from-an-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-798">Ottenere dati da un'app</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-798">Obtain data from an app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-799">Se un'app è in grado di rispondere alle richieste, è possibile ottenere dati sulle richieste, le connessioni e altri dati dall'app tramite middleware inline di terminale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-799">If an app is capable of responding to requests, obtain request, connection, and additional data from the app using terminal inline middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-800">Per altre informazioni e codice di esempio, vedere <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-800">For more information and sample code, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-801">App lenta o sospesa (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-801">Slow or hanging app (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-802">Un *dump di arresto anomalo* del sistema è uno snapshot della memoria del sistema e può contribuire a determinare la provocazione di un arresto anomalo dell'app, dell'avvio o dell'applicazione lenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-802">A *crash dump* is a snapshot of the system's memory and can help determine the cause of an app crash, startup failure, or slow app.</span></span>

#### <a name="app-crashes-or-encounters-an-exception"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-803">Arresto anomalo o eccezione di un'app</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-803">App crashes or encounters an exception</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-804">Ottenere e analizzare un dump da [Segnalazione errori Windows](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-804">Obtain and analyze a dump from [Windows Error Reporting (WER)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-805">Creare una cartella per i file dump di arresto anomalo del sistema in `c:\dumps`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-805">Create a folder to hold crash dump files at `c:\dumps`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-806">Il pool di app deve avere accesso in scrittura alla cartella.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-806">The app pool must have write access to the folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-807">Eseguire lo [script di PowerShell EnableDumps](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-807">Run the [EnableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-808">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting in-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *w3wp.exe* :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-808">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe* :</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps w3wp.exe c:\dumps
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-809">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting out-of-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *dotnet.exe* :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-809">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe* :</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps dotnet.exe c:\dumps
     ```

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-810">Eseguire l'app nelle condizioni che causano l'arresto anomalo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-810">Run the app under the conditions that cause the crash to occur.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-811">Dopo che si è verificato l'arresto anomalo, eseguire lo [script di PowerShell DisableDumps](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-811">After the crash has occurred, run the [DisableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-812">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting in-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *w3wp.exe* :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-812">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe* :</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps w3wp.exe
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-813">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting out-of-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *dotnet.exe* :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-813">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe* :</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps dotnet.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-814">Dopo l'arresto anomalo di un'app e la raccolta dei dump, l'app può terminare normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-814">After an app crashes and dump collection is complete, the app is allowed to terminate normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-815">Lo script di PowerShell configura Segnalazione errori Windows per raccogliere fino a cinque dump per ogni app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-815">The PowerShell script configures WER to collect up to five dumps per app.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-816">I dump di arresto anomalo del sistema potrebbero richiedere una grande quantità di spazio su disco (fino a diversi gigabyte ognuno).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-816">Crash dumps might take up a large amount of disk space (up to several gigabytes each).</span></span>

#### <a name="app-hangs-fails-during-startup-or-runs-normally"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-817">L'app si blocca, si verifica un errore durante l'avvio o viene eseguita normalmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-817">App hangs, fails during startup, or runs normally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-818">Quando un'app si *blocca* (smette di rispondere ma non si arresta in modo anomalo), si verifica un errore durante l'avvio o viene eseguita normalmente, vedere [file di dump in modalità utente: scegliere lo strumento migliore](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) per selezionare uno strumento appropriato per produrre il dump.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-818">When an app *hangs* (stops responding but doesn't crash), fails during startup, or runs normally, see [User-Mode Dump Files: Choosing the Best Tool](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) to select an appropriate tool to produce the dump.</span></span>

#### <a name="analyze-the-dump"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-819">Analizzare il dump</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-819">Analyze the dump</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-820">È possibile analizzare un dump usando diversi approcci.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-820">A dump can be analyzed using several approaches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-821">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file) (Analisi di un file dump in modalità utente).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-821">For more information, see [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span></span>

## <a name="clear-package-caches"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-822">Cancella cache di pacchetti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-822">Clear package caches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-823">Un'app funzionante potrebbe non riuscire immediatamente dopo l'aggiornamento del .NET Core SDK nel computer di sviluppo o la modifica delle versioni del pacchetto all'interno dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-823">A functioning app may fail immediately after upgrading either the .NET Core SDK on the development machine or changing package versions within the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-824">In alcuni casi i pacchetti incoerenti possono interrompere un'app quando si eseguono aggiornamenti principali.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-824">In some cases, incoherent packages may break an app when performing major upgrades.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-825">La maggior parte di questi problemi può essere risolta attenendosi alle istruzioni seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-825">Most of these issues can be fixed by following these instructions:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-826">Eliminare le cartelle *bin* e *obj* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-826">Delete the *bin* and *obj* folders.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-827">Cancellare le cache dei pacchetti eseguendo [le impostazioni locali di DotNet NuGet All--Clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) da una shell dei comandi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-827">Clear the package caches by executing [dotnet nuget locals all --clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) from a command shell.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="129cd-828">La cancellazione delle cache dei pacchetti può essere eseguita anche con lo strumento [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) e l'esecuzione del comando `nuget locals all -clear` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-828">Clearing package caches can also be accomplished with the [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) tool and executing the command `nuget locals all -clear`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-829">*nuget.exe* non è un'installazione inclusa con il sistema operativo desktop Windows e deve essere ottenuta separatamente dal [sito Web NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-829">*nuget.exe* isn't a bundled install with the Windows desktop operating system and must be obtained separately from the [NuGet website](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-830">Ripristinare e ricompilare il progetto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-830">Restore and rebuild the project.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-831">Eliminare tutti i file nella cartella di distribuzione nel server prima di ridistribuire l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-831">Delete all of the files in the deployment folder on the server prior to redeploying the app.</span></span>

## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-862">Errori di avvio dell'app</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-862">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-863">In Visual Studio, per impostazione predefinita, un progetto ASP.NET Core viene [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) host durante il debug.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-863">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-864">Un *errore del processo 502,5* che si verifica quando è possibile diagnosticare localmente il debug usando i consigli in questo argomento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-864">A *502.5 Process Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-865">403,14 non consentito</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-865">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-866">Non è possibile avviare l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-866">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-867">Viene registrato l'errore seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-867">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-868">L'errore è in genere causato da una distribuzione interruppe sul sistema host, che include uno degli scenari seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-868">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="129cd-869">L'app viene distribuita nella cartella errata del sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-869">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="129cd-870">Il processo di distribuzione non è riuscito a spostare tutti i file e le cartelle dell'app nella cartella di distribuzione nel sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-870">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="129cd-871">Il file di *web.config* non è presente nella distribuzione oppure il contenuto del file di *web.config* non è valido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-871">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-872">Seguire questa procedura:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-872">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-873">Eliminare tutti i file e le cartelle dalla cartella di distribuzione nel sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-873">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-874">Ridistribuire il contenuto della cartella di *pubblicazione* dell'app nel sistema host usando il normale metodo di distribuzione, ad esempio Visual Studio, PowerShell o la distribuzione manuale:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-874">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-875">Verificare che il file *web.config* sia presente nella distribuzione e che il relativo contenuto sia corretto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-875">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-876">Quando si esegue l'hosting in app Azure servizio, verificare che l'app venga distribuita nella `D:\home\site\wwwroot` cartella.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-876">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-877">Quando l'app è ospitata da IIS, verificare che l'app venga distribuita nel **percorso fisico** IIS visualizzato nelle impostazioni di **base** di **Gestione IIS** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-877">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager** 's **Basic Settings** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-878">Verificare che tutti i file e le cartelle dell'app vengano distribuiti confrontando la distribuzione nel sistema di hosting con il contenuto della cartella di *pubblicazione* del progetto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-878">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-879">Per ulteriori informazioni sul layout di un'app ASP.NET Core pubblicata, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-879">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-880">Per ulteriori informazioni sul file di *web.config* , vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-880">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-881">500 - Errore interno del server</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-881">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-882">L'app viene avviata, ma un errore impedisce al server di soddisfare la richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-882">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-883">Questo errore si verifica all'interno del codice dell'app durante l'avvio o durante la creazione di una risposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-883">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-884">La risposta potrebbe non avere alcun contenuto o essere visualizzata nel browser come un codice *500 Errore interno del server* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-884">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-885">Il log eventi dell'applicazione in genere indica che l'app è stata avviata normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-885">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-886">Dal punto di vista del server, questo è corretto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-886">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-887">L'app è stata effettivamente avviata, ma non può generare una risposta valida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-887">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-888">Per risolvere il problema, eseguire l'app dal prompt dei comandi nel server o abilitare il log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-888">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-889">502.5 Process Failure (Errore del processo)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-889">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-890">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-890">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-891">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-891">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-892">Il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta di avviare il processo di lavoro, ma l'avvio non riesce.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-892">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-893">In genere è possibile determinare la causa di un errore di avvio del processo dalle voci nel log eventi dell'applicazione e nel log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-893">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-894">Una condizione di errore comune è dovuta alla configurazione non corretta dell'app perché come destinazione viene specificata una versione del framework condiviso ASP.NET Core, che non è presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-894">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-895">Controllare le versioni del framework condiviso ASP.NET Core installate nel computer di destinazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-895">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-896">Il *framework condiviso* è il set di assembly (file *DLL* ) che vengono installati nel computer e cui fa riferimento un metapacchetto, ad esempio `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-896">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies ( *.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-897">Il riferimento del metapacchetto può specificare una versione minima richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-897">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-898">Per altre informazioni, vedere [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/) (Il framework condiviso).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-898">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-899">La pagina di errore *502.5 Errore del processo* viene restituita quando il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo a causa di un errore di configurazione dell'hosting o dell'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-899">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-900">Non è stato possibile avviare l'aggiornamento dell'applicazione. Errore: 0x800700c1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-900">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-901">L'app non è stata avviata perché non è stato possibile caricarne l'assembly ( *.dll* ).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-901">The app failed to start because the app's assembly ( *.dll* ) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-902">Questo errore si verifica quando è presente una mancata corrispondenza del numero di bit tra l'app pubblicata e il processo w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-902">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-903">Verificare che l'impostazione del pool di app a 32 bit sia corretta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-903">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-904">Selezionare il pool di app in **Pool di applicazioni** di Gestione IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-904">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-905">Selezionare **Impostazioni avanzate** in **Modifica pool di applicazioni** nel pannello **Azioni** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-905">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-906">Impostare **Attiva applicazioni a 32 bit** :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-906">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications** :</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-907">Se si sta sviluppando un'app a 32 bit (x86), impostare il valore su `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-907">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-908">Se si sta sviluppando un'app a 64 bit (x64), impostare il valore su `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-908">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-909">Verificare che non esista un conflitto tra una `<Platform>` proprietà di MSBuild nel file di progetto e il bit pubblicato dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-909">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-910">Connection reset (Connessione ripristinata)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-910">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-911">Se si verifica un errore dopo l'invio delle intestazioni, è troppo tardi perché il server possa inviare un codice **500 Errore interno del server** quando si verifica un errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-911">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-912">Questo spesso accade quando si verifica un errore durante la serializzazione di oggetti complessi per una risposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-912">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-913">Questo tipo di errore viene visualizzato come un errore di *reimpostazione della connessione* nel client.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-913">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-914">La [registrazione delle applicazioni](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) può consentire di risolvere questi tipi di errori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-914">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-915">Limiti di avvio predefiniti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-915">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-916">Il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) è configurato con un valore predefinito di *startupTimeLimit* di 120 secondi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-916">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-917">Quando si mantiene il valore predefinito, l'avvio di un'app potrebbe richiedere fino a due minuti prima che il modulo registri un errore del processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-917">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-918">Per informazioni sulla configurazione del modulo, vedere [Attributi dell'elemento aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-918">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-919">Risolvere i problemi relativi al servizio app Azure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-919">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-920">Registro eventi applicazioni (servizio app Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-920">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-921">Per accedere al log eventi dell'applicazione, usare il pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** nel portale di Azure:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-921">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-922">Nel portale di Azure aprire l'app in **Servizi app** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-922">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-923">Selezionare **Diagnostica e risoluzione dei problemi** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-923">Select **Diagnose and solve problems** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-924">Selezionare l'intestazione **Strumenti di diagnostica** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-924">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-925">In **Strumenti di supporto** selezionare il pulsante **Eventi dell'applicazione** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-925">Under **Support Tools** , select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-926">Esaminare l'errore più recente dalla voce *IIS AspNetCoreModule* o *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* nella colonna **Origine** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-926">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-927">Un'alternativa all'uso del pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** consiste nell'esaminare direttamente il file del log eventi dell'applicazione usando [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-927">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-928">Aprire **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **Strumenti di sviluppo** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-928">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-929">Selezionare il **pulsante &rarr; Vai** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-929">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-930">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-930">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-931">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-931">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD** .</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-932">Aprire la cartella **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-932">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-933">Selezionare l'icona della matita accanto al file *eventlog.xml* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-933">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-934">Esaminare il log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-934">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-935">Scorrere fino alla fine del log per visualizzare gli eventi più recenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-935">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-936">Eseguire l'app nella console Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-936">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-937">Molti errori di avvio non producono informazioni utili nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-937">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="129cd-938">È possibile eseguire l'app nella console di esecuzione remota [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) per individuare l'errore:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-938">You can run the app in the [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki) Remote Execution Console to discover the error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-942">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-942">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD** .</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-943">Test di un'app a 32 bit (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-943">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-944">**Versione corrente**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-944">**Current release**</span></span>

1. `cd d:\home\site\wwwroot`
1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-945">Eseguire l'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-945">Run the app:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-946">Se l'app è una [distribuzione dipendente dal framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-946">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

     ```dotnetcli
     dotnet .\{ASSEMBLY NAME}.dll
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="129cd-947">Se l'app è una [distribuzione autonoma](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-947">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

     ```console
     {ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-948">L'output della console dall'app, che visualizza gli eventuali errori, viene inviato tramite pipe alla console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-948">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-949">**Distribuzione dipendente dal framework in esecuzione in una versione di anteprima**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-949">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-950">*Richiede l'installazione dell'estensione del sito del runtime ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-950">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x86) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-951">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` è la versione di runtime)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-951">`cd D:\home\SiteExtensions\AspNetCoreRuntime.{X.Y}.x32` (`{X.Y}` is the runtime version)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-953">L'output della console dall'app, che visualizza gli eventuali errori, viene inviato tramite pipe alla console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-953">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-64-bit-x64-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="129cd-954">Test di un'app a 64 bit (x64)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-954">Test a 64-bit (x64) app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-955">**Versione corrente**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-955">**Current release**</span></span>

  1. `cd D:\home\site\wwwroot`
  1. <span data-ttu-id="129cd-959">Eseguire l'app: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-959">Run the app: `{ASSEMBLY NAME}.exe`</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-960">L'output della console dall'app, che visualizza gli eventuali errori, viene inviato tramite pipe alla console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-960">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-961">**Distribuzione dipendente dal framework in esecuzione in una versione di anteprima**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-961">**Framework-dependent deployment running on a preview release**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="129cd-962">*Richiede l'installazione dell'estensione del sito del runtime ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64).*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="129cd-962">*Requires installing the ASP.NET Core {VERSION} (x64) Runtime site extension.*</span></span>
